https://github.com/X9Developers/block-explorer/commit/e5e7d1715cbd8cd3197455b69fab82cbc66fdf27
commit e5e7d1715cbd8cd3197455b69fab82cbc66fdf27
Author: Alexis Hernandez <alexis22229@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Sep 22 07:48:54 2019 -0600

    server: Migrate database from TXID_TYPE to HASH_TYPE
    
    The change reduces the disk usage considerably because TXID_TYPE is a TEXT while
    the HASH_TYPE is a byte array.
    
    This reduces around 25% disk requirements on XSN, on BTC that's hundreds of gigabytes.
    Be aware that applying this evolution will take a while on production.

https://github.com/X9Developers/block-explorer/commit/26b005c527cc5951024f1795d3e98954182e4a82
commit 26b005c527cc5951024f1795d3e98954182e4a82
Author: Alexis Hernandez <alexis22229@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Aug 16 22:09:56 2019 -0600

    server: Initial schema migration from hex strings to bytes
    
    The HEX_STRING_TYPE is deleted and BYTEA is used instead, which
    only stores the bytes instead of the hex-string representation.
    
    The merkle_root column is changed from TEXT to BYTEA.
    
    The transaction_outputs.hex_script column is changed from TEXT to BYTEA.
    
    The disk requirements for these fields is reduced by half.

Author: Alexis Hernandez <alexis22229@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed Feb 27 21:33:28 2019 -0700

    server: Filter out duplicated transactions while synchronizing the ledger
    
    Bitcoin allows duplicated transactions that are already spent, this causes
    conflicts when retrieving them from the txindex because the older ones are lost.
    
    Filtering the lost transactions reduces the consistency but allows to keep syncing.

Author: Alexis Hernandez <alexis22229@gmail.com>
Date:   Sat Mar 30 21:21:47 2019 -0700

    server: Synchronize the TPoS contracts
    
    - A TPoS contract is created when the transaction is synchronized.
    - A TPoS contract is deleted when the transaction is rolled back.
    - A TPoS contract is closed when the collateral output is spent.
    - A TPoS contract is enabled when the collateral output gets unspent.
